et saut fuers li dolor, si com nos avons dit en l’aposteme dou foie.	and he will burn with fire, as we have said in the word of the liver.
Mais en cestui ovraige est paour ou li malaides muert maintenant, ou fistule i vient qui ne puet estre sanee.	But in this work there is fear or the patients die now, or a fistula comes that cannot be healed.
de la mice	of the abscess.
Quant tu cures la maladie de la mice de ceu que nos avons dit as divisions des cures, et il ne profite mie, adonques i afierent III manieres de cautere que tuit sont boin.	When you treat the disease of the abscess as we have said about the divisions of the treatments, and it does not profit at all, then they mention three kinds of cautery that are all good.
Desquelz li une maniere si est que tu faices III cauteres, ou IIII, en lignant selonc la longor de la mice, selonc la figure dou cautere dou foie que nos avons dit devant;	From which one is a certain way so that you make three cauteries, or four, binding according to the length of the mouse, according to the figure of the liver cautery that we have said before.
et n’apresser mie ta main a tout le cautere, et soit li malaides sovins sor son dos;	and do not press with your hand at all the cautery, and let the sick man lie on his back;
et une autre maniere de cautere si est que tu eschaufe le cautere qui a II ners, si com nos l’avons mostreit en la dislocation de l’espaule;	and another way of cautery is that you draw the cautery with two nails, as we have shown in the dislocation of the shoulder;
et lieve le keur qui est endroit la mice, ou li coutes dou malaide vient devers senestre, et soit li elevations dont tu lieves le keur selonc la keur, selonc la longesce dou cors, et li cautere soient selonc la largesce dou cors.	and lift the wound which is towards the mouse, or if the cuts of the sick person come to the left side, and so that the elevations you lift according to the wound, according to the length of the body, and the cautery are as wide as the breadth of the body.
Aprés i boute les II ners enflamez tant que li keurs soit perciez de l’autre part, et puis trai fuers le cautere, et ensi en i avra IIII.	After the two fingers are burned, they should be flamed until the pain is perceived from the other side, and then take fire to apply cauterization, and thus it will have four effects.
Et se tu vues, si cauterize a tot le cautere a III ners.	And if you see that all the cauterization is with three fingers.
Aprés le cure quant il a geteit porriture par lonc tens, et ce vaut mues que li autre des cures devant dites.	After the treatment when it has been exposed to rot for long times, and this applies to those who have already received other treatments said before.
de ydropisie	Of dropsy (or edema).
Cautere ne vaut a ydropique, fors c’a la maniere qui est apelee «asclytes».	Cautery is not effective for dropsy, except when applied in the manner known as "asclytes".
Quant tu la cures selonc les manieres que nos avons dit en divisions, et ta cure ne profite mie, adonques covient il que tu li faices IIII cauteres entor la boude, et I sus l’estomac, et un sus le foie, et I sus la mice, et II derrier le dos sus l’espinee, et I endroit le pis;	As you cure according to the manners that we have said in divisions, and if your treatment does not benefit, then it is necessary to make four cauterizations between the nostrils, and one above the stomach, and one above the liver, and one below the mice, and two behind on the spine on the spine, and one on the opposite side of the foot.
et soit li cauteres bien pres de l’espés dou keur.	and if the cauterizations are well near the spot of the wound.
Aprés laisse le cautere aovert por giter porriture lonc tens, et ne lassier mie la cure dou malaide aprés le cautere;	After leave the cauterization to be open for a long time, and do not leave the patient's cure after the cauterization.
et sanation se hasterait, et seront ensamble les II ententions avec l’aide de Deu.	and healing would hasten, and there will be two intentions with God's aid.
Li forme dou cautere por le ventre soit li clavile que nos avons devant mostreit;	The form of the cautery for the belly is the claw which we have shown previously;
et cil por le dos soit olivaire, selonc ceu qu’il est ci devant mis.	and that for the back is olive oil, as has been shown previously.
de l’enfleure des piez	of swelling of joints.
Quant li piez sont enflez a celui qui est ydropique, et sont plain d’awe citrine, il covient que tu cauterizes sus le dos dou piet entre l’auriculaire et l’anulaire;	When the feet are swollen in one who is dropsical and filled with dewy citron juice, it is necessary to cauterize on the back of the foot between the auricle and the ankle;
et lieve ta main avec le cautere sens torner.	and lift your hand with the cautery towards turning.
Et n’entrer mie trop em parfont, ensi sarrait fuers li awe citrine, et soit li cauteres selonc cest forme:	And do not enter too deeply in this method, lest they suffer like the one who was burned by fire, and so should you use cauterization according to this form:
Aprés fai sus II jambes II cauteres en chescune jambe a la pointe dou cutellaire;	After, make two cauterizations in each knee, one in the toe of the cutlass-shaped knife.
et soit li cauteres dou lonc, l’un desoz le genoil devant et l’autre defuers, enmi la jambe;	and let them cut open to the long one, on both sides of the knee.
et laisse les cauteres aovers longement sens curer, que li awe en isse;	and leaves the cuts open for a long time to be treated, until they heal.
aprés le cure des autres cures que nos avons dit.	after treating other treatments that we have said.
de la menoison	of the house.
Quant solution de ventre vient de froidor et de moistor, tant que li vertus retentive et digestive qui est ou stomac et en l’intestine est afleboie, et ne puet estre curez par manieres de cures;	When a belly disorder comes from cold and moisture, so that the retained virtues and digestion that is in the stomach and intestines are deficient, and cannot be cured by other treatments.
et tu vois le malaide bien soffrant et de fort vertut, si fai I grant cautere sus l’estomac selonc ceu qu’il en a parleit ci devant ou cautere de l’estomac, au cautere circule;	and you see the patient suffering much and having great weakness, so do a cautery on the stomach according to what he said before, or stomach cautery, in circular motion.
et IIII cauteres entor la boude subtilz a tout I cautere clavile subtil, et II cauteres sus les hainches.	and four fire cauteries are to be applied near the subtle nerves, and two fire cauteries are to be applied on the veins.
Et se tu vois les moistors habundans et le malaide soffrant, se li fai cautere sus le poignil, et I cautere sus chaicun yle, et II petis cauteres sus l’estomac delez le grant, car li cure est profitans quant il i a bone aide.	If you see the moistors abundant and the patient suffering, make fire cautery on the nail, and do fire cautery on each joint, and two cauteries on the stomach with the great one, because the cure is beneficial when it has good aid.
de la cure des emorroydes	About the treatment of hemorrhoids.
Quant les emorroydes sont ou fondement, ou une ou plusors, et sont ancienes et sont de grosses humors froides et moistes corrumpues, et sont curees si com nos avons dit en divisions, et il ne profite mie, si fai cauteres:	When the ulcers are on the fundament, or one or more of them, and they are old and are swollen with gross humors that are cold, moist, and corrupted, and they are treated as we have said in divisions, but it does not profit, then apply fire cautery:
III sus l’espine dou dos, celi qui est tout defuers desoz almecdate poc et poc en triangulant, et I cautere desoz la boude II dois;	Three times on the spine of the back, those who are behind the almeccade, a little by a little in a triangle shape, and two fire cauteries below the nerves.
et se tu penses que ses estomac soit refroidiez, et li viande ne cuise, et on voit enfler la faice, adonques li faice on I grant cautere sus le stomac, si com il est devant dit, et I autre sus le foie, et I autre sus la mice a tout le cautere clavile;	and if you think that the stomach is cold and the flesh does not cook, and the face swells up, then apply one fire cautery on the stomach, as it has been said, and one more above the liver, and one more above the spleen with all the cauterization clavile.
et laisse le cautere overt lonc tens.	and let the fire cautery be left on for long periods.
Aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez.	After a cure, the limb must be made sound again.
de la charnositeit qui est nommee «thelul»	of the fleshiness which is named "theleul
Quant tu copes althelul, si eschaufe le cautere qui semble I raseur, et puis le met tout embraseit sus cel althelul copeit;	When you apply the cautery to the ulcer, if it seems as if the fire is making the sawing motion of a razor, and then put it completely ablaze on the ulcer that has been cut.
et i laisse tant ta main que li cauteres viegne a la naissance de la voine, de coi li sans cort;	and leave it so long that the fire comes to the root of the vein, because there is no cutting.
fai ceu une fois ou II, et s’il i a mout d’althelul, si cauterize chaicun si com nos avons dit;	do it once more and if there is much of the ulcer, cauterize each part as we have said.
aprés les cure d’oignemens profitans tant qu’il soient sanez;	after the application of ointments, which are beneficial until they become healthy.
et se tu cauterizes d’un cautere grant sus alchatim, si avra plus grant aide.	and if you apply a great fire to the swollen part, it will have more relief.
de plaie mal curee	of badly treated wounds.
Quant li malaides ne puet soffrir tailleure ne overture, que nos raconterons en son leu, si vient teil maladie que ne puet estre sanee fuer que par cautere.	When the patient cannot bear either a dressing or an opening, that is what we will tell in his case, if it comes to such a sickness that can only be cured by cautery.
Quant a aucun vient fistule, et est enveillie et giete porriture et moistors corrumpues, si la doies prover a tot une tente subtil, et garde que tu saiches a tot la tente combien elle a de parfont.	When there is no fistula, and it has grown old and swollen with putrefaction and moist corruption, if you wish to prove the depth of the wound, and guard so as to know how far it goes.
Aprés eschaufe le cautere qui semble I raseur, et le boute en la fistule selonc la quantiteit que li tente i est entrée, et rencomence lou cautere tant que cil cors porris et corrumpus soient ars, une fois, ou II ou III, selonc la quantiteit de som besoing;	After the cauterization that resembles a razor, and pour it into the fistula according to the quantity that has entered, repeatedly perform the cautery until the corpse is burned and corrupted once, twice, or three times, depending on how much it needs.
et te warde d’ardre lé nerf qui sunt enqui, et des grans voinnes.	And be careful of the ardent nerve that is inflamed, and great veins.
se li fistule vait au cors de la vesie et a l’intestine, si te warde de ces leus, et ne faire ceu fuers que en leu charnut, et pense qu’ele n’est mie persans;	If the fistula is in the abdominal cavity and intestine, be careful with those things, and do not apply fire to them unless in the gallbladder, and think that they are not human.
aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez, et se li leus est saielez, et les matieres sont ostees lonc tens, adonc saiches que li leus est sanez entierement;	After treating the animal so that it is made whole again, and if the intestines are swollen, and the materials are long time stored, then you know that the intestines are made whole.
et se les matieres ne sont ostees, saiche que li leus est troez, et corrumpus li os au font;	And if the materials are not bones, then know that the limb is rotten, and corrupting the bone to the point.
et ensi com un de ces que nos dirons en son leu.	and thus as if we were speaking on its behalf.
de la maladie des reins	of kidney disease
Quant dolor de froit vient as rains, et de grosse ventositeit, et ne prent talant de femme, adonc covient il que tu li fais cautere sus les rains d’une part et d’autre au cautere clavile que nos avons devant dit;	When a pain of frost comes from the rain, and a great swelling, and it does not take hold in the woman, then it is fitting that you make fire cautery above both sides of the affected area and with the barbed needle which we have previously mentioned.
et se nos le cauterizons em mileu, si avra III cauteres en ligne, et se feront plus grant aide.	and if we cautery in the middle, then there will be three fire cauteries in line, and these will bring greater relief.
de la vessie	of the bladder
Quant li vessie est mole et foible de froit et de moistor, si que li malaides retient l’urine, adonc li fai cautere en la partie defuers sus la vessie, la ou encomencent li poil dou poignil, et I a destre et I a senestre, et soit chescuns cauteres si lons com li nous d’un poce;	When the bladder is weak and damp from frost and moisture, and the patient retains urine, then you must cauterize in the area behind the bladder, where the hairs grow at the navel, on both sides, and one on each side, so that both are cauterized as long as one point.
et li fais I cautere defuers le dos, ou II se tu en as besoing;	And let the fire cautery be performed on the back, where it is necessary.
et soit li cauteres clavile selon la forme devant dite.	and let the fire cautery be performed on the clavicle according to the shape described.
de la marris	of the marrow
Quant li marrix est froide et moiste, et ne laisse mie por ceu a concevoir, et les flors sont corrumpues et lor termines tarde;	When the marrow is cold and moist, and does not allow for conception, and the flowers are corrupted and their ends are late.
et quant elles vienent, si sent grant dolor:	and when they come, they cause great pain.
adonques covient il c’on li faice III cauteres entor la boude, si com nos avons dit ou cautere de la vessie, et II cauteres defuers le dos;	so it is necessary to perform the fire cautery inside the womb, as we have said about fire cautery of the bladder, and also on the back.
et soit li cauteres clavile, si com nos avons dit.	and let it be performed on the clavicle, as we have said.
de la hainche	of the joint
Quant les moistors viscouses dessendent a la boiste de la hainche, et por ceste cause si se muet de son leu, et li signes est que li cuisse est plus longe que li autre quant on le mesure ensamble;	When the mucous viscera descend into the joint of the haunch, and because of this they move out of their place, and the signs are that the thigh is longer than the others when measured together.
et est trovez li leus dou departement vuis, si covient que tu cauterizes le malaide sus la boiste de la hainche a I cautere semblant au cercle, et seigne devant le leu entor la boiste si com elle torne, si que li boiste soit dedens le cercle;	and it is found in the joints from departure by moving around, so it is fitting that you cauterize the patient under the skin of the hawthorn branch as if to draw a circle, and hold before the joint as if it were turning, so that the skin is inside the circle;
et si soit li cauteres telz com cil dont on a cauterizeit le stomac.	and if it is so cauterized as those which have been cauterized of the stomach.
Et se cist cauteres ne t’est presens, se li fai III cauteres de l’olivaire grans, et soit li cauteres ausi parfont com tous li keurs;	And if these cauterizations are not present, then do three cauterizations of the olivary branch, and make them as thick as all the keys.
et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	and heal him until he is made whole.
de la dolor de la hainche	of the pain of the groin
Quant dolor vient en la boiste de la hainche, et c’est de froidor et de moistor, et li malaides est curez de ceu que nos avons dit en la division et li cure ne vaut, et li maladie est anciene:	When pain comes to the skin of the hawthorn branch, and it is from cold and moisture, and the patient is cured by what we have said in the division, but the cure does not work, and the illness is ancient.
adonc covient il que tu purges le malaide des grosses humors de pilules fetides, ou autres pilules bones semblans.	Then it is necessary to purge the patient of the heavy humors of old, foul pills, or other hard pills.
Aprés li fai cautere;	After applying the fire cautery;
et li maniere dou cautere si est selonc II manieres:	and it is done according to two manners:
c’est a savoir ensamble medicines ardans, et cautere de feu.	which means assemble medicines with herbs, and fire cautery.
Cautere de feu si est selonc mout de manieres, desquelz li uns est telz:	Fire cautery is according to many ways, of which some are like this:
que tu cauterize sus la boiste de la hainche III cauteres triangulalz selonc ceste forme, et i fai bone profunditeit et grant, et ait entre chaicun cautere d’espaice la groissece d’un doi, et soit li cauteres olivaire;	Where you cauterize on the bark of the juniper tree, three cauteries in the triangular form, and make it deep and large, and space each cauterization as wide as a doves egg, and are olive oil cauteries;
aucune fois fait on cautere en mileu sus lou chief de la hainche, por coi il en i a IIII selonc ceste forme:	Never is cautery performed in the middle of the cheekbone, because there are four kinds according to this form:
Et se tu vues, si le cauterize au cautere dou cercle que nos avons devant dit en la dislocation de la hainche;	And if you see, if the cautery at the point of a circle that we have said in the dislocation of the cheekbone;
mais fai en teil maniere que li cercles conteigne toute la hainche, et tous li espés dou keur soit ars.	but do it in such a manner that the circle contains all of the cheekbone, and all the bone in the area where it was burned.
Et c’est li maniere c’on fait en sciatique, quant li dolor tient en la hainche, et ne parvient mie jusc’a la cuisse ne jusc’a la jambe.	And this is the manner in which one does it when applying the sciathe (a form of treatment), as the pain stays in the hamstring and cannot reach either the thigh or the leg.
Et s’ele vient jusc’a la cuisse et la jambe, se li fai II cauteres lai ou li malaides dit que li dolor li tient, et I cautere desus la cheville IIII dois, a la partie senestre un poc;	And if it comes close to the thigh and leg, make two cauteries above where the patient says that the pain is, and four doves, on the right side a little.
et soit li cauteres cutellaire, et soit arse li espesseté dou keur;	and whether it's the cutlass cautery or burn the thicker bone.
et se li malaides sent que li dolor s’estende jusc’a dois dou piet ou pres d’enqui, se le cauterize la ou il sent la dolor III poins ou IIII au cautere qui est apelez «poins».	and if the patient feels that the pain is spreading to both of two feet or near it, then you should apply the cautery at the place where he feels the pain three times or four times which is called "point".
Et se mestiers est, se li en fai plus;	And if it happens that they do more.
et se il seit que li dolor soit desoz le genoil vers la cuisse, se li fais cautere au cautere cutellaire ou circulaire, et te done bien garde en tous tes cauteres que tu n’i lassier mie tant le cautere que tu brules les ners et les grans arteres, et que tu ne faices au malaide plus grant nuisance et contraction.	and if he feels that the pain is below the knee towards the thigh, then you should apply the cautery at the cutellaire or circular cautery; and well guard in all your cauteries so that you do not burn the nerves and great arteries too much, and do not cause the patient greater nuisance and contraction.
Et je meisme ai veus plusors qui ont fait cautere sus la cheville dou piet, et li lasserent tant que li jambe fut toute enflee, et li piez ausi, et fut perciez et corrumpus toz li piez.	And I myself have seen others who did fire cautery on the ankle of the foot, and they burned so much that the leg was completely swollen, and the toes as well, and it became consumed and corrupted all the toes.
Aprés une solution de ventre dont il ot la mort.	After a stomach solution in which he died.
Et se li dolors est en II parties ensamble, fai cautere en l’une et en l’autre, selonc ceste maniere.	And if the pains are in both legs together, do fire cautery in one and the other, according to this manner.
Et li saige dirent en la cautere de la hainche, de coi ci est li maniere, fai I tel fer et soit au chief ausi gros com uns nauvillon de dacte, ou un poc moins, et soit par entrechetres et soit des l’un entrechetres jusc’a l’autre d’espaice la quantiteit d’un nou de poce;	And the wise men said in the cautery of the hawthorn because this is the way, make an I such iron and it should be as big as a sailor's finger or slightly less, and so between each other with the space of an arrowhead to the quantity of a piece of thread.
et soient li entrechetres aovers de II pars, et soient aussi comme noez, et i ait I mainche de fer bien fait;	and they shall be joined together again of two parts, and shall also be like now, and there shall be one bolt of iron well-made;
et c’est li forme:	and this is the shape:
Et soit eschaufez tant qu’il soit toz rouges et giete senteles, et puis le mette on sus la boiste de la hainche malaide, et soit tornez sus lou sain costeit;	And so it should be heated until it is completely red and smells like vinegar, and then put upon the bone of the sick patient, and turned onto the healthy side;
et lou cauterize une fois I cautere reont et lou laisse III jors;	and after the cautery is done once again they shall leave it for three days;
et puis fai emplaustre de burre, et laisse la plaie aoverte lonc tens;	and then cover with butter and let the wound be covered for a long time;
aprés la cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	after the bandaging treatment until it is healthy.
Albucasim dit que nos usons poc de cest cautere por la paor de son regart, et se voions poc qui en usent;	Albucasis says that we should use it little because of the fear of its sting, and since few people have used it;
et toutevoie ceu est des boins cauteres, qui le puet soffrir, et lai ou il s’afiert.	and it is clear that this is a good cautery, which he can bear, and where he is treated.
Li cauteres de medicine ardant si est que tu faices I estrument a entrechetres en coi dessende li marge de la porte, et soit d’arain ou de fer a une paroit longe, et en la hautece ait II nous, et ait entre chaicun la quantiteit de la groissece d’un doi;	The cautery of medicine is hot so that you make an instrument between the channels in which it falls on the margin of the door, and it is either of iron or of steel with a long appearance, and at its top there are two of each size and quantity, corresponding to the thickness of a dole.
et soient overt defuer et desus, et se joignent ensamble selonc ceste forme:	and are put over and above, and join together according to this form:
Aprés met sus la boiste de la hainche au malaide gisant sor suin costeit sain, et apresse ta main mout sus la boiste de la hainche;	After putting the blade of the hazelwood on the patient lying on his side, and pressing your hand very strongly onto the blade of the hazelwood.
aprés giete entre les II cercles de l’awe chaude qui soit chaufee au feu I poc, et li laisse une houre dou tens, et soffre li malaides la chalor et l’arsure de li.	After placing between the two circles of hot ash which are heated by one pot, and letting him suffer for one hour in bed, and feeling the heat and the burning of him.
Car il i trueve mordication ausi com de feu;	It occurs from biting as well as from fire;
et quant li mordications iert passee, se lieve ta main avec l’estrument et leve la hainche d’awe douce, et laisse ensi III jors, et met sus burre tant que ceu qui est noir de l’eschaudure soit osteit;	And when the bite has passed, lift up your hand with the instrument and gently lift the heel of the foot, and let it be for three days, and put on butter until the blackness of the bruise is healed.
et lou laisse III jors que porriture en istrait;	and let it be for three days so that putrefaction will cease;
et ceu serait li derriene aide aprés le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	And this would be the rear part healed after the treatment of ointments until it is fully recovered.
Et se li dolor s’est estendue jusc’a la cuisse ou jusc’a la jambe, se li fai I estrument que teigne awe selonc ceu que tu as fait en la hainche igaument;	And if the pain has extended up to the thigh or down to the leg, make an instrument that tightens more than you did in the heel.
et c’est li maniere de l’awe chaude, et je l’ai escripte ou traitier de la rectification de medicine.	and this is the method of applying hot ointment, and I have written it to treat the art of medical correction.
Pren alcali et chaulz vive, autant de l’une com de l’autre, et les broie ensamble, et les met en I nuef pot.	Take alum and vinegar alive, equal quantities of each, and grind them together, and put them in a new pot.
ou il ait I petit pertuis defuer se que li pointe d’un raisor i puisse entreir;	If there is a small opening made beforehand so that the point of an arrow can enter.
et met desor celui pot I autre pot bien plombeit, et met sus alcali et chalz et awe douce sus, tant qu’il en i ait I doi desus les poudres cant tu l’avras bien preingte a ta main;	And put a second pot with another kind of lead or silver on it, and add vinegar and gall and apply the powder to it so that when you have two layers of them over the wound, you will be able to grip it firmly in your hand.
et le laisse ensi tant qu’il en dessende awe ague et chiece ou pot plombeit, puis pren toute cele awe, et la giete sus chalz et sus alcali si com devant.	And let it remain in that state until the fever and pus descend from the opening of the lead or silver pot, then take out all of it, and apply gall and vinegar to it as before.
Et lors si sera mout ague et est aministree en mou d’ovraiges de medicine et en cauteres d’autres membres.	And if the fever is severe and has been brought under control through application of various medicines and cauterizations on other parts of the body.
Car elle fait auteil oevre com feus, et si a autres medicines dont on cauterize bien la hainche ensi com tesisie et miel anacardi et chalz avec savon, toutes ces choses mellees ensamble.	For it does all sorts of work like fire, and there are other medicines that must be cauterized well, such as this mixture of treacle, honey from the acacia tree, gall with soap.
Et Galiens nos raconte une cure dont uns hons fut curez de la dolor de la hainche et de la voine sciatique, et lou loe mout, et dit que on n’i fist autre cure, et qu’il en fut sanez a une soule fois quant on ot fait ceste cure, et il se fut baigniez si com il l’enseigne ci aprés.	And the Galen tells us of a cure in which one man was cured of the pain of the vein and sciatic pain, and great praise for it, and he says that there was no other cure needed, and he became whole once after this cure, and he bathed himself as he teaches it here afterwards.
Et dist en teil maniere que tu preignes dou litargire vert fres et sec, et le broie mout avec I poc de graisse, et met sus la hainche et sus la cuisse et sus la jambe ou la dolor tient, et la lie;	And instruct the patient to press with a firm and fresh green leaf, and grind it much with a little fat, and put on the haunch and on the thigh and on the leg where the pain is felt, and bind.
et li laisse III houres et par la quantiteit que li malaides ne sente plus l’arsure.	and let him leave three hours and by the quantity that the patient feels no more of the burning.
Et puis le fai entrer ou bain tant que li cors li soit un poc arousez, et lou fai entrer ou lit, et li dolor s’en ira toute et sera sanez.	And then put it into a bath until the body is slightly swollen, and put it into the bed, and the pain will go away entirely and be healed.
Et saiches que nuls ne doit user de cautere de telz medicines, se ceu n’est aprés l’evacuation de cors.	And knows that no one should use cauterization with such medicines unless it is after the evacuation of blood.
Et Dyascorides dist que quant li voine sciatique est cauterizee de fiens de chievre, si i aide mout;	And Dioscorides says that when the varicose vein is cauterized with horsehair, it will greatly aid.
et doit estre fais li cauteres en teil maniere.	and must be done in this way.
Prenez lainne et la beurez d’oile vielz, et metez sus la fossete qui est entre le pouce dou piez et l’autre qui est apelez foscile.	Take a linen cloth and anoint it with old oil, and place it on the fossa which is between the big toe and the small toe.
Aprés pren fiens de chievre sec, et l’empren a feu tant qu’il soit charbons, et lou met sus la laine, et le laisse tant qu’il soit estains;	After taking dried horsehair and wrapping it in fire until it is charcoal-like, and then put it on linen, and let it be so stained;
et refai encor ensi, et ne cesser de faire ensi tant que tu penses par sens qu’il viegne jusc’a la hainche, et que li dolor soit cessee;	and redo again, and do not stop doing so until you think with sense that it comes to the heat, and that the pain is ceased;
et cist manieres de cautere est apelez «cautere de chievre».	and this method of cautery is called "cautery on the knee".
de la dolor dou dos	of the great pain in the back.
Quant dolor vient au dos, ou par cheoir ou de percussion ou par trop grant evacuation, ou par semblans de matiere espandue froide, a nule de ces semblances ne vaut cauteres, fuer que a celi qui vient de infusion de froide matiere.	When pain comes to the back, whether by falling or by percussion, or by great evacuation, or because it seems like material is spread out cold, none of these symptoms are worth cauterizing, except for those who come from an infusion of cold matter.
Il covient c’aprés ceu que li malaides est voidiez de pilules fetides ou d’autres semblans, que on li faice sus lou dos, lai ou li dolor tient, trois lignes signies d’enche, et en chescune ligne V cauteres ou plus selonc la vertut et la quantiteit que li malaides puet soffrir;	it is necessary after this that the patient is void of fetid pills or other similar things; and on his loin, in that place where the pain lies, three lines signed with cautery, and in each line one or more according to the virtue and quantity that the patient can bear;
et soit fait li cauteres selonc le cautere qui est apelez «poins»;	and let it be done the cautery as is called "points".
et se tu vues, fai III cauteres ou IIII au cautere clavile moien selonc ceste forme:	and if you see, do three cauteries or four on the cauterized joint in this form:
Maintes fois vient ceste maladie as petis enfans, et li signes de l’encomencement si est qu’il ont estroite alainne quant il se lievent, et paor;	This is often the case with this illness in small children, and the signs of its beginning are that they have a stiff neck when they lift it up, and fear.
et tu trueves en la derriene espinee dou dos et en nous l’apparance qui vient sus les autres espinees.	and you find in the lower back spine and on your back the appearance that comes above the other spines.
Quant tu vois ceu et tu le vues curer, si le cauterize au cautere de celcle selonc ceste forme.	When you see this and you see them being cured, if you cut him with the cautery of a cell according to this form.
Si que li cautere porpreigne chescune partie de l’espinee egaument.	So that the fire cautery affects each part of the spine equally.
Et se tu vues, si cauterize entor l’espinee au cautere poignant II lignes ou III, et soient li poins pres l’uns de l’autre.	And if you see that when the fire cautery cuts into the spine at two or three points and the wounds are close together.
Aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez selonc ceu que nos avons dit, et warde que tu n’amenistrer cautere en gilbositeit qui soit en spame de nerf.	After treating the patient so that he is healthy again as we have said, and take care not to apply fire cautery in gangrene which has inflammation of nerve.
de la dolor des jointes	of pain from the joints.
Quant dolor de jointes sunt de moistors que sont espandues a chaicun membre dou cors, et quant dolor vient em piez, que li mire apelent «podagre» proprement, et quant elle est de froide cause et cures de medicines ne la puent curer, si est curez par cauteres en teil maniere:	When pain in joints is caused by moist spots that have spread to each limb of the body, and when pain comes to the foot, they call it "podagre" properly, and since it's caused by cold reason and medicines cannot cure it, if cured by cautery in this manner:
fai li mout de cauteres entor la jointure dou piet, et soit li cauteres olivaire selonc ceste forme:	cut the oil of cauterization into the joint of the foot, and make the cauterization according to this form:
Et s’il i a besoigne que tu poignes sus la faice dou piet, se li fai cautere a tot le cautere c’on claime «point».	And if he has need to prick at the flesh of the foot, then let him perform fire cautery on all the cautery as we claim "a point".
Et se les dolors viegnent jusc’a genous et as autres jointures, et ceu avient maintes fois, se li fai cautere sus chaicun genoil III cauteres ou IIII de chescunne partie, a tout le cautere olivaire;	And if the pains come to both knees and other joints, and this has happened many times, then for each knee three cauteries or four of each part, all of these olive cauteries.
et se tu as mestier de plus, si en fai plus, mais n’i tenir mie ta main fuers que tant que li espés dou keur soit ars.	and if you have more business to attend to, so do it more, but do not keep your hand wet until the spices are dried.
Et se les dolors dessendent jusc’a genoil et au dos, se li aministre le cautere que nos avons dit en son chapistre.	And if the pains descend just to the knees and back, let him administer the cautery as we have said in this chapter.
Et se les dolors sunt as mains, si fai poins entor le foscile II lignes;	And if the pains are in the hands, so make points on each side of the wrist two lines.
et s’il remaint point de dolor as dois, si fai poins sus chescune jointe et sus lou poil de la main;	and if there is no pain in the fingers, make points on each joint and on the hair of the hand;
et se les dolors vienent jusc’as coutes ou jusc’as espaules, si cauterize chescune partie, et fai boin governement au malaide et penre medicines.	and if the pains come to either elbows or shoulders, cautery each part, and give good governance to the patient and administer medicines.
Car se tu li fais boin governement et tu purges fleume, si sera saneis a l’aide de Deu.	If you do good governance and purge the phlegm, so will you be cured by God.
de la routure dou syfac	From the work of the cauterization
Quant routure vient en angres, et li bouelz dessendent as coions et c’est novelement, si covient que quant tu lou vues curer, qu’il ne menjuce mie celui jor;	When a fracture comes with blood, and the bowels descend into the joints and it is newly so, then you must not treat it on the same day.
et qu’il use choses qui laichent lou ventre, si que li fiens dessende de son ventre;	and that he uses things which make the belly swell, so that the fumes come down from his belly.
aprés le fai seoir sus son dos entre tes mains, et li comande qu’il teigne son alaine tant que li boueil soient repairiet, et les ramoinne a tes dois, et seigne d’enche desoz la routure sus l’os dou poignil, et a tout un signe que soit semblans a la moitiet d’un cercle a desus dou cors;	After you make him sit on his back between your hands, and he orders you to tighten his leg so that the bowels are repaired, and take hold of it, and sign with ink on both sides of the fracture on the bone at the joint, in such a way that it is similar to half of a circle above the body;
puis eschaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	then takes out the cauterizing instrument for this purpose:
tant qu’il soit blans et qu’il giete senteles.	As long as they are white and senselessness.
Puis ramoine les bouels a lor leu;	Then takes out the bowels to their place;
et li ministres teigne sa main sus qu’il ne retornent arrier;	And the attendants keep their hand above you so they do not return to your back;
et oevre bien les cuisses au malaide, et met desoz lui I cussin et I serjant sus les cuisses, et I autre sus lou pis qui li teigne les mains;	And work well on the thighs of the patient, and put a cloth over his crotch and another over his groin to keep his hands from being bruised;
puis met le cautere sus lou signe a tout ta main, et lou tien droit et lou tien tant que tu ateignes l’os, et se tu ne l’ateins la premiere fois, si le rencomence encor une autre tant que tu viegnes jusc’a l’os;	then put the cautery on the mark at all your fingers, and hold tight with one hand and steady with another until you strike the bone, and if you do not strike it the first time, then repeat it again as many times as necessary until you reach the bone.
et te warde subtilment que li boueil ne saille quant tu fais lou cautere;	and beware subtly lest the boiling blood escapes while you are doing the cautery;
que tu ne le brulasses;	lest you burn it.
et que par ceu li malaides ne muere, ou autre malz.	and that the patients may not die from this or another illness.
Et saiches que quant tu ne viens jusc’a l’os au cautere, tes ovraiges ne vaut rien.	And know that when you do not come to the bone with the cautery, your work is worthless.
Et covient que li cauteres des enfans soit subtilz selonc la mesure d’ous, et des grans gens aussi grans selonc lor mesure;	It is necessary to treat children with subtlety according to their measure; and great people as well in proportion to their size.
aprés III jors cure lou leu dou cautere de burre tant que li eschaudure soit ostee;	After three days of treatment with butter cautery, until the scab is fallen.
aprés le cure d’autres oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez, et gise li malaides XL jors sus son dos tant que li plaie soit bien soudee;	After the treatment of other ointments until he is cured, and applying the patient for 40 days on his back so that the wound is well dressed.
et covient que ses norrissemens soit lassatis longement, si que li boueil ne saillent quant il se preigdra d’aler en chambres.	and it is necessary that his nourishments be prolonged for a long time, so that the boils do not burst when he gets up to walk in the chambers.
Et aprés XL jors, quant il se voudra lever, se li amenistre une faixe bien faite, et la porse XL autres jors;	And after 40 days, when he wishes to rise, apply a well-made bandage and wear it for another 40 days;
et ait boin repos, qu’il se travaille poc et se warde de trop grant repletion de boivre et de mengier, et de trop haut braire;	and let him have good rest, he must work little and be careful not to drink too much wine and meat, and eat too high.
et quant il fait cest enseignement si est sanez entierement.	and when he follows this instruction so is entirely healed.
Et je dirai ci aprés la cure de taillier en son chapistre.	And I will say this after your operation on cutting with a cautery.
de la routure dou ventre	of the operation on the stomach
Quant routures vienent en autres ventres et sont connisans, et tu vues qu’elles ne croissent plus, se li fai I cautere dou cautere reont selonc sa quantiteit, et soit ars li tiers dou keur;	When gashes come in other parts and are discovered, and you see they no longer grow, then do the fire cautery according to its quantity, and cut off one-third of the cure.
aprés le cure selonc ceu que nos avons dit;	after the treatment as we have said;
et aucun des anciens ont dit c’on le doit cauterizer au cautere a III angles selonc ceste forme:	and none of the ancients have said that you should do the cautery with three angles according to this form:
mais signe premier le leu d’enche et fai une ligne per la largesce desus la routure, et une autre defuers, et main ta main emmi a tout le cautere clavile.	but first mark the size of the opening in the incision, and make a line for its width, and with your thumb press all around the cautery nail.
Mais li premiers cauteres est plus legiers et muedres.	But the first cauteries are lighter and more gentle.
de dolor anciene en aucun membre	Of old pain in any limb
Quant dolor vient en aucun membre, ou de cheoir ou de ferir, et cele dolor tient lonc tens, et li cure de medicine n’i vaut, adonc covient qu’il soit cauterizeis au cautere qui est apelez «poins», et soit li cauteres selonc la longesce dou membre et la petitece et sa foibleteit et sa vertut et sa location de torcions et de sa dolor.	When pain comes to any limb, whether from a fall or an injury, and that pain persists for a long time, and the medicine cure is not helpful, then it is necessary to cauterize with the cautery called "poins", and do the cauteries according to the length of the limb and its smallness and weakness and its virtue and its location of twists and its pain.
s’il est sanez dou premier cautere, c’est bien;	if he is healed after the first cautery, it is well;
se ceu nom, recomence I autre cautere sus celui, car teilz costume est qu’il se doit muer au membre que li est prochiens, por coi il covient que tu faices les cauteres tant que li malaides soit saneis.	For the head of the shoulder, instruct the patient to repeat another cauterization on that one, because this treatment is suitable for the movement of the limb that is next to it, so you must do the cauterizations until the patient becomes well.
de meselerie	Of clumsiness or ineptitude
Li meseil sont aidiet aucune fois par cautere par grant aide, et meismement li maladie que vient de la putrefaction de fleume et de melancolie.	The problem is not helped by cautery for a great amount of time, and the disease itself that comes from the rotting of pus and melancholy.
Cant tu la vues cauterizer, pren warde se li maladie est au comencement, et s’ele est curee selonc ceu que nos avons dit en la division, et ne dessent ne ne demoure, et tu doutes que li corruption ne porpreigne tout le malaide, adonques li fai V cauteres sus lou chief:	Can you see the cauterizer, take care if the patient is at the beginning of an illness, and if they are cured according to what we have said in the division, and do not cut or remain still, and doubt that corruption will spread throughout the entire body, then make cauterizations on the head.
I emmi le chief a nouf, et l’autre vers lou front a la fin des chevous;	Emboss the head again and the other side of the forehead to the end of the eyebrows.
et II sus les II cornes, et I derrierre sus le haiterel;	and also on the two horns, and one behind the ear.
et i laise tant ta main que li cauteres viegne jusc’a l’os, et tant que les escorces en issent fors si que les vapors des grosses humors s’en puissent issir;	And I let your hand stay so that the cautery comes to life just before the bone, and so long as the scabs come out in great numbers, so that the vapors of the large humors can come out.
et le cauterize sus la mice selonc ce qu’il est devant.	And cut off the mouse according to what it is in front of.
Et se li meselerie est partout esparse;	And if the meshing (of tendons) is everywhere sparse;
et elle pert manifestement, si covient que tu lou cauterizes de ces cauteres que nos avons dit ou chief, et I cautere en som lou neis, et II cauteres sus l’espinee dou col, et VI cauteres sus l’espinee dou dos, et I grant sus la crupie et I autre delez, et II sus les II espaules;	and if it is manifest that it pertains, so it is advisable to cut with these cauterizations which we have mentioned before, and cutting some in the neck, and two on the spine of the back, and one on the shoulder, and one on the elbow, and two on the other shoulders;
et II sus les coutes, et II sus les tendrons dou pis, et I sus chascune jointe des mains et des piez, et sus les fosses des mains;	and two on the groins, and two on the tendons of the leg, and one on each joint of the hands and feet, and on the hollows of the hands;
et te warde des ners que sunt sus lou derrien calcant, que tu ne les bruler;	And warn yourself of the nails that are under the nostrils, lest you burn them;
et aucune fois fait om cautere sus l’os dou poignil, et I autre sus l’os de l’estomac, et I autre sus lou foie.	And at no time perform cautery on the bone of the finger joint, and another on the bone of the stomach, and another on the liver.
Et saiches que quant plus i fais de cautere, plus li fais d’aide, et mues li profite;	And know that when you do more cautery, the more benefit it brings.
et saiches que li malaides ne sent point de dolor au cautere si com li sain le sentent, por ce que li cors est ja toz corrumpus.	And know that the sick do not feel pain from cautery as much as they who are healthy do, because the body is already completely corrupted.
Et covient ke li cautere soient grant et petit selonc les membres et les jointures, selonc ceu que vos lou troverez en manieres des fers.	It is necessary that the cautery be large or small according to the members and joints, as you will find in various iron instruments.
Aprés cure lou leu de farine de veces avec miel et autres cures tant qu’il soit saneis.	After treating him with the lead of flour mixed with honey and other remedies until he is cured.
Quant enfleure vient en aucun membre et est curee par medicines et oiles et emplastres, et il n’est mie sanez, adonques li fai cauteres sus le membre selonc la grandour et la petitece dou membre;	When an inflammation comes upon any member and is cured by medicines and oils and plasters, and it is not healed, then you should perform cautery on the member according to its size and smallness.
et soit li cauteres un poc entrans en l’espés dou keur;	And let the cauteries be made a little further in, when he is lying in expectation of pain.
puis le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	and then the treatment of ointments until he is healthy again.
Et aucune fois fait on cautere et a la main et au piet et au dos, a l’issue dou nerf que muet le membre, et ensi si est ostee li enfleure;	And sometimes cautery is done by hand and with the knife and the foot and the back, at the end of the nerve that makes the limb mute, and so if it has an abscess.
et toutevoie ne s’en entremette nuls s’il n’est conoissans des membres et des issues des ners movans lou cors.	and no one should enter into it unless he knows the limbs and the ends of moving nerves in the body.
de albaras	of wounds.
Quant li maladie qui est apelee «albaras» est enveillie, et li engien de medicine n’i valent rien, adonques le cauterize d’un cautere un poc parfont, selonc la quantiteit de l’espés dou keur, tant que li blenchour soit ostee, et soit muee sa color;	When the sickness called "albaras" is old and worn out, and medicine will not do anything for it, then cauterize with a cautery just enough to pierce to the bone, according to the quantity of pain felt, until the blenchour (i.e. the swelling) is removed, and the color changes.
puis le cure de farine de veces et de lentilles avec oile roset et foilles de plantain, et sanc de colon et sanc d’alondre, de chescun une partie;	Then apply the treatment of flour, of fenugreek and lentils with olive oil and leaves of plantain, and blood from colon and gall of goose, one part each;
et soit mellez tout ensamble, et soit liiez d’un drapel, et soit aers au leu tant qu’il soit sanez.	and then let it all be melted together, and tie it with a cloth, and apply to the patient as long as they are healthy.
li cure de chancre par cautere	The treatment for the chancre by fire cautery
Quant chancre vient au comencement, et tu lou vues arrester, si le cauterize au cautere qui semble I cercle, tout entor au tour dou chancre.	When the chancre first appears and you want to stop it from growing, if you burn it with fire cautery, around the entire circle of the chancre.
Et toutevoie li saige dirent que on faice cautere ausi au mileu dou chancre;	And all wise men say that you should apply fire cautery also to the middle of a carbuncle;
et toutevoie ceu ne me semble mie boin, car je redous que il ne soit ulcerez et corrumpus, et je l’ai ja veut avenir aucune fois;	And all wise men seem to me not good, because I fear that it will cause ulceration and corruption, and I have never wished for such an event;
et plus droituriere chose est qu’il soit cauteriés entor, au cautere qui est apelez «circule», si com nos avons dit en mout de cauteres.	and the most reliable thing is to cauterize within, at the cauterization called "circle", as we have said in many other cauterizations.
de l’enfleure qui ne puet meurer	of the inflammation which cannot be killed
Quant aucuns ait une maladie qui est apelee «adubelati», et elle tarde de meurer ou por la superfluiteit qu’ele fait ou por l’eaige dou malaide quant il est decrepites (c’est a dire trop vielz) et il a poc de sanc, ou por lou tens;	When some have a disease called "adubelati", and it lingers until death or because of the superfluity that she makes or because of the old age of the sick person when he is decrepit (this means too much old) and he has little blood, or for long time;
et tu la vues haster de meurer:	and you must see it hasten to death:
adonques le cauterize entor de mout de petis cauteres en poignant;	so therefore cut into the root of a small cautery in pricking.
aprés le laisse ensi.	then leaves it thus.
Car elle se hastera de meureir.	It will happen to die.
Et se tu la vues percier a tout le cautere, si chaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	And if you see it pierced with the cauterization at all, then this heat will be the form:
Et met ta main en mileu de cele maladie qui est apellee «adubelati» tant que li cauteres ait perciet lou keur, et soit telz li cauteres que li malaides lou sente defuers en teil maniere que li cours de la porriture soit alegis.	And place your hand at the middle of that illness called "adubelati" until the cauterization pierces the vein, and so arrange the cauterization that the patient feels pain in that manner that the course of the putrefaction is delayed.
Aprés le cure tant qu’il soit sanez parfaitement.	After the treatment until it is completely healed.
li cure dou feu par fer	the cauterization with iron.
Une autre maniere de maladie i a qui est apelee «corrodens», et n’est autre chose que une mengeson de membre, car ele menjut les membres ausi com li feus les leignes seches.	Another kind of illness that is called "corrodens", and it's nothing but an infection of a member, because it corrupts the flesh just as fire burns.
Se tu vois ceste maladie en leu qui puisse soffrir cautere ensamble feu, adonques eschaufe les cauteres clavile mout petit et grant, selonc ceu qu’il covient au leu ou li maladie est;	If you see this disease in the one who can suffer fire cautery, then take out small and large nails according to what is fitting for the patient or the disease.
aprés le cauterize de toutes pars tant que tu erraiche toute la corruption, et nen remaigne rien de li, que tout ceu qui est corrumpus ne soit osteit.	After cautery of all parts until you have eradicated the entire corruption, and nothing remains, then all that which is corrupted should be removed.
Et puis le laisse III jors, et met sus les leus cauterizez soffre broiet avec oile tant que les eschaudures dou feu soient ostees, et toute li corruption.	And then leave it for three days, and put on the patient's cauterized wounds so that they suffer bruising with oil until the scalded areas are cut out and all the corruption.
Aprés lou cure d’oignemens engendrans char.	After this treatment, generated from the use of medicines.
Et se tu vois aprés III jors que chars saine ne naisse, c’est boin;	And if you see after three days that a healthy child does not appear, it is good;
et se ceu non, si rencomence le cautere sus ceu qui est demoreit des leus corrumpus.	and if that does not happen, then reapply cauterization to those who are left corrupted.
Et ceste mengeson est aucune fois esteit curee de medicine ague en leu de cautere de feu;	And this method is never cured with medicine or water in place of cauterization by fire;
mais toutevoie cautere de feu est de plus grant aide, et j’ai ja dit la cure de la medicine ague en la division:	but cauterization by fire is of greater aid, and I have already said the treatment with medicine in division:
pren la quant tu en as mestier.	take as much as you need.
des porrelz qui vienent as piez	of porridge that comes from the bones
Mout de fois avient que as piez par defuers naist une maladie qui est apelee «clos» selonc nostre entencion, et est une grosse chose fautree qui blece lou piet.	Many times, from the bones due to lack of care, a disease called "closure" occurs according to our understanding, and it is a serious thing that causes great pain.
Et li cauteres de ceste maladie si est selonc II manieres.	And the fire cauteries for this disease are according to two ways.
C’est a savoir cautere de feu, et cautere d’aigue chaude.	That is to say, fire cautery and hot water cautery.
Cautere de feu si est que tu eschaufe I cautere cheveit ausi com est une penne de vouteul, et soit fait de boin fer a la mesure qu’il puisse porpenre le clou de toutes pars, et qu’il i ait subtilz marges;	Fire cautery is that you should stuff a caul (a membrane) like an egg with wool, and it be made of good iron to the measure that can pierce through all parts, and have subtle edges;
aprés le met tout chaut sus lou clou, et torne ta main tot entor le clou tant qu’il viegne au font dou clou;	After that put the head on the nail, and turn your hand around the nail so it comes out from the nail hole;
et lou laisse ensi III jors tant qu’il encomence giter porriture;	and let him wait for three days so that he begins to get purulent matter;
puis li fai un emplaustre de malves savaiges broiies avec seil, et laisse l’emplaustre sus toute la nuit, et li clous cherra et sera desracinez de ses racines.	Then make a poultice of fresh marrows crushed with string, and put the poultice on the whole night, and the nail will come out and be loosened from its roots.
Puis cure le leu d’oignement enjanrant char tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then treat the joint with puncture and care until it is clean.
Et s’il sont convertit par defuers lou cors, et maintes fois avient et en mains et em piez, si covient que tu i amenistres cautere d’aigue chaude;	And if they are converted in flesh, and it often happens in hands and feet, then it is advisable to apply fire cautery of hot water;
et est en teil maniere:	and it is thus:
pren une cainne d’arain ou de fer, ou une penne de vouteul, et met sus lou clou et l’althelul, c’est asavoir porrelz verrues;	Take a needle of iron or thorn, and set the nail on it is to say, to prick warts;
et met la cainne sus si qu’ele porpreigne tout entor, puis i met un poc d’awe chaude, et retien bien ta main, et presse ta main en tornant si que li marge de la cainne viegne a la racine dou clou, et puisse trover l’aigue chaude voie parfonde jusc’a la racine;	and then set the needle on it so that it pricks all around; and then put a little warm water on it, and hold well your hand, and press hard with your hand turning so that the margin of the needle comes to the root of the nail, and you can find the warm water running deep just to the root;
et soffre li malaides un poc la mordication de l’aigue chaude une houre;	and let the patient suffer a little from the burning of the warm water for an hour;
puis le laisse ensi, et il se derracinera tous a tout ses racines.	and then he will drop off all its roots.
Ensi fai un aprés autre, tant que tu esraiches toz ces qui sont au cors, puis les cure des oignemens qui engenrent char.	So let the hair grow after another, until you are searching all those who are in the body; then treat with ointments that inflame the flesh.
li cure dou trembler	the treatment of trembling
Quant aucuns tremble de froidor de ners, ou de fievre quartaine ou d’autre, si covient que tu li faices IIII cauteres ou IV sus l’espinee dou dos, I cautere entre chescune espinee;	When some people shiver from cold or from fever or from another, so you should make four cauteries or four above the spine of the back, one cautery between each spine.
et I cautere ou pez, et I sus l’estomac au cautere olivaire;	and one above the belly at the olive cautery;
si laissera lou trembler, et se hastera li santez de la maladie froide.	so that it will stop trembling, and hasten the recovery of the patient from the cold disease.
des pustules puans	of festering pustules
Aucune fois apperent par defuers le cors bathes, ou pustules puans, que vienent de grosses matieres corrumpues.	Never do they appear by chance on the body without baths or festering pustules, which come from gross, corrupted matter.
si covient au premier quant eles apperent que on faice cautere sus chescun chief de la pustule:	if it is fitting to do so at first when they appear that you make cautery on each head of the pustule;
un cautere subtil de fust de mirte, de coi li pointe soit emprise au feu, ou de racine de aristologe longe, ou au cautere lenticulaire.	a subtle cautery of fusel of myrtle, so that the point is gripped by fire, or from the root of aristolochia long, or at the cautery lens.
Et aucune fois les cauterize on au comencement quant il aperent, selonc ceste maniere, et il ne puent croistre des enqui en avant, mais est desrompue li superfluitez dont il vienent, et sont sanez;	And sometimes when cautery is applied at the beginning and they see this manner, but they cannot increase in size or grow forward, but instead burst the superficial swellings that come from it, and are healed.
mais il covient que ceu soit fait aprés l’evacuation de sanc.	but it is necessary that this be done after the evacuation of blood.
quant li artere est copee	when the arteries are cut
Maintes fois avient grans decorremens de sanc de l’artere qui est copee a la plaie que vient au pardefuers, ou a l’incision de l’aposteme, ou au cautere dou membre, et as semblans choses;	Often great bleeding comes from the artery that is cut at the wound, or at the incision of the abscess, or by cauterizing the member, and similar things.
et est mout grief chose d’estenchier.	and it is a very grievous thing to stink.
Et toutevoie quant ceu avient a aucun, si te haste de mettre ton doi indice sus la plaie de la voinne, et l’estrain mout tant que li sans soit apaisiez desoz ton doi, et que goute n’en isse plus;	And whenever this happens to anyone, if you hasten and put your two fingers on the wound of the vein, and stretch it very much so that the pain does not pass away, and no more bleeding comes from it,
puis met au feu les cauteres olivaire plusors petis et grans tant qu’il soient tuit rouge;	Then put on fire the cauterization oils many small and large ones until they are all red;
puis empren I, ou grant ou petit selonc la plaie et lou leu en coi li artere est route, et met le cautere sus cele voine ou tu tiens ton doi, et tien le cautere tant sus que li sans soit restainchiez.	Then apply one, or great or small according to the wound and as to where the artery is cut, and put the cauterization on that vein where you hold your thumb, and keep the cauterization there until the blood stops flowing.
Et s’il saut fuers quant tu lieves ton doi desus la voinne, et li cauteres estint, si pren hastivement I autre des cauteres qui sont au feu.	If the fire escapes when you lift your thumb over the vein, and the cauteries are extinguished, then take it hastily another of the cauteries that are on fire.
Et ne cesser de faire ceu l’un aprés l’autre tant que li sans soit estenchiez;	And do not cease to apply that one after another until the blood stops flowing.
et warde que tu n’ardes lou nerf qui est delez, et que autre malice ne viegne sus lou malaide;	and beware that you do not burn the nerve which is near, and that no other harm befalls the patient.
et saiches que quant sans decourt de l’artere, c’on ne lou puet mie bien restenchier meismement quant li artere est grans, se ceu n’est par une des IIII manieres que nos avons dit:	and know that when the artery is cut without bleeding, it cannot be properly closed itself when the artery is large, unless this is one of the four ways we have mentioned.
ou par cautere, ou par extraction quant ele n’est mie traite, ou par fort liement de fil, ou par medicines mises sus qui ont pooir de restenchier sanc;	In order to treat with fire, or by extraction when it has not been treated, or by binding tightly with thread, or by medicines placed on which have the power to stop bleeding;
et soit liee et estrainte avennament.	and if it is bound and strained as a result.
Qui i amenistrera restenchement de liier estroitement de drapelz ou de metre choses ardans sus, ou autres semblans choses, se n’i profite se poc non.	Who will put on a restraint of tight binding with cloth or tying things tightly above, or other similar things, unless it does not benefit.
Et se ce avient a aucun et il n’ait mie mire ne medicine present, si doit mettre son doi indice sus la plaie de la voinne si com nos avons dit, et bien estrendre tant qu’il soit restenchiez desus la plaie et desus la voinne;	And if this happens to no one and he has not taken any medicine or remedy, then he must put his two fingers on the wound of the vein as we have said, and bind them tightly until the bleeding is stopped from the wound and from the vein.
et ne remuer lou doit, mais lou moille d’awe froide sovent que soit mout froide tant que li sans soit congelez et engrossiez et restenchiez;	and he must not move it, but the cold from his hot blood will often cause it to become very cold, until its heat is frozen and condensed, and stopped.
et faice des enqui en avant ceu dont il a mestier de cauteres et de medicines.	and seek to cure and remedies those who need it.
Ci encomence li secons livre des cures de taille	This begins the second book on treatments of wounds.
Nos vos avons dit ou premier chapistre toute maladie en coi il covient cautere de feu, ou de medicine ardans, et les oquisons et les causes et les estrumens et les formes des cauteres;	We have said this in the first chapter of all diseases in which it is necessary to apply fire or medicine hot, and the qualities and causes and the strumas and forms of cauteries;
et ai mis celui chapistre des lou chief jusc’a piez, et je irai en cest chapistre par celi meisme voie por ceu c’on trueve plus legierement ceu c’on voura.	and the head of that chapter is as follows, and I will go into this same place for the same reason, because it heals more easily when found in the same place.
Et ainsois que je encomence ceu, il covient, chier fil, que vos aprenez que en cest chapistre a plus de peril et de paor que ou premier des cauteres, et por ceu il covient plus grant cautele.	And so that I begin this, it is necessary, dear child, that you learn that in this chapter there is more danger and fear than with the first cautery, and therefore you must be more cautious.
Car en l’ovraige de cest chapistre avient maintes fois evacuation de sanc a l’ovrir la voinne, et a l’incision sus aposteme, et as cures des plaies, et a l’estraction des saiettes, et a l’incision sus la piere, et les semblans choses;	For in the work of this chapter there are often evacuations of blood when opening a vein, and incising an abscess, and in the treatment of wounds, and in the extraction of arrows, and in cutting into stones, and similar things; where there is doubt and fear, and many die.
ou il a doutance et paor, et en vient li mors a plusors.	where there is doubt and fear, and many die.
Et je vos amoneste que vos n’entreprenez folie.	And I warn you not to act foolishly.
Car mout de manieres de gens vienent en cures.	For many kinds of people come in for treatment.
si vienent de telz qui s’aïrent si avec lor maladie qu’il muerent legierement por la forsenerie qu’il trueve de sa maladie, et de la grandour de son malice;	When they come from such people who are afflicted with their disease so that they quickly die because of the hardness they find of their disease, and of the greatness of their misfortune;
et de ces doit on avoir paor.	and from these, one should have fear.
Et de ces i a qui te done son sens, et dit:	And of those who tell you the truth, and say:
«atendez, je sui garis»;	wait, I am cured".
et li maladie est despitouse.	and the disease is stubborn.
Il ne covient mie que vos vos consentez a ces qui vienent a vos qui ont ceste maniere, mais mettez plus grant cusanson en vostre honor qu’en vostre covoitise, et n’ovrez mie folement mais saigement de ceu dont vos estes certain, et dont vos poez avoir pris et los;	It is not good to trust only those who come to you and have this condition, but take greater caution in your honor than in your desire, and be firm without being feeble, of that which you are certain, and of what you can acquire.
et usez de pronostication et de indication en cures de vos malaides a coi salus soit convertie;	And instruct the patient with prognosis and diagnosis to determine when their health will change;
et ceu vos aidera a aquester bone renommee, et gloire, et memoire de loenge.	And this will help you gain fame, honor, and memory of praise.
Tres chier fil, Nostres Sires vos doint boin entendement et droiture, et se vos vuelle espireir de la sainte inspiration de sa main, amen.	Three dear children, Our Lords give you good understanding and integrity, and if you wish to aspire to the holy inspiration of His hand, amen.
Or je vos ai ordeneit cest chapistre en devisant par chapistres, selonc ceu qu’il est devant ou chapistre des cauteres, que je vos ai deviseit des le chief jusc’a piez, por ceu que vos trovez plus legierement ceu dont vos avrez mestier.	Or I have ordered this chapter in the form of chapters, according to what is before or behind a cautery chapter, which I have devised for you from the head right down to the foot, because you will find it easier to know those things that you will need.
dou chief plein d’aigue	The full head is filled with water.
Saiches que ceste maladie vient mout de fois as enfans a l’enfanter, et quant li baille estraint trop fort le chief de l’enfant;	Know that this disease comes often to children when they are born, and when the nurse holds the child too tightly around the head;
et aucune fois vient ceu de cause reponue que on ne seit.	And sometimes it comes from a cause that is not known.
Et je ne vis onques ceste maladie fuers qu’en enfans, et a toz ces que j’ai veus se hastait li mors;	And I have never seen this disease except in children, and all those who I have seen have died.
et por ceu me semble qu’il me vaut mues lassier l’ovraige en teilz cures.	And therefore it seems to me that I should try a few of these treatments.
Et je vis I enfant de coi li chiés estoit plains d’aigue, et li chief engroissoit chescun jor tant qu’il ne lou pooit sostenir;	And I saw that child because his shoulder joint was swollen with water, and his head became increasingly heavy every day until he could no longer bear it;
et crut tant li moistor qu’il fut mors, et ceste moistor si est assemblee desoz l’os sus lou syphac, entre lou keur et l’os;	and he thought so greatly that he was dead, and this moisture had assembled itself under the bone above his spleen, between the kidney and the bone;
et li ovraiges si est telz se li moistor est entre lou keur et l’os, et li apostemes est petis, que tu fendes emmi lou chief une fendure large;	and the wounds are so serious when the moisture is between the kidney and the bone, and the abscesses are small, that you must cut a large incision in his head;
et soit ausi longe com II nous, tant que li mostor corre;	and it should be as long as ours, so that the moisture may run.
et vez ci la forme dou spatumile:	and in this case, the form of a spatula;
Se li moistor est plus creue, et li aposteme soit plus grans, si fai II fendures en maniere d’une croix, selonc ceste forme:	If the moisture is more crusted and the abscesses are larger, then make two incisions in the shape of a cross, according to this form:
Et se li moistor est desoz l’os, et li signes que tu vois les commissures dou chief overtes de chescune partie, et li aigue saut fuer quant tu la presses de ta main au dedens, et ceu ne t’est mie reponut:	And if the moisture is under the bone, and you see the signs that there are cracks in both sides of the head, and the water spurts out when you press with your hand inside, and it does not come back;
si covient que tu fendes enmi lou chief III fendures selonc ceste maniere:	If you must cut open his skull three times, according to this manner:
Et aprés l’incision estrai la moistor toute fuers.	And after the incision extract all the moisture completely.
Aprés estraint les fendures de drapelz et de poudres, et i met vin et oile, et laisse ensi jusc’a cinquieme jor;	After fastening the incisions with bandages and powder, and applying wine and oil, and leaving them so for five days;
puis le deslie, et cure la plaie par tentes et par oignemens, et laisse estraindre le chief egaument, et done mengier au malaide viande seche de poc de moistor tant que li membre soit confortez et sanez.	then remove the dressing, and treat the wound with poultices and ointments, and let the head be strained in size, and then give the patient dried meat of a few ounces of moisture until the limb is comforted and healed.
Et une autre maniere d’incision est que tu regardes ou apert li grandor de l’aposteme, et li assemblé de l’aigue;	And another manner of incision is that you observe or open the large opening of the abscess, and assemble the assembly of water;
car aucune fois est elle devant;	because it will never be seen;
aucune fois derrier;	nor behind;
aucune fois en destre;	Never once.
et aucune fois en senestre.	and never on the left side.
Taille donques lai ou li aposteme apert, et l’emplissement de l’aigue, et lou fent selonc ce que tu en as le pooir;	Therefore at the size or at the abscess opening, and the filling of the liquid, and the cutting accordingly as you have the power;
et warde que tu ne coper l’artere;	and beware that you do not cover the artery.
et veigne flun de sanc, si que li malaides muere dou decorrement de sanc et de l’evacuation de moistor.	and if there is bleeding, so that the patients die from the decay of blood and the evacuation of moisture.
de reume	The head of the shoulder
Quant il avient a aucun une maladie qui est apelee «catarre» as eulz ou au pis, et li maladie est anciainne, et li cure de medicine ne profite mie, adonques li derraine cure si est li cauteres avec ceu c’on li copera les II arteres.	When it happens that a person suffers from a disease called "cataract" in the eyes or at the worst, and the patient is old, and medical treatment does not work, then the last resort is to cut with cautery using what they will cut off both arteries.
Il covient donques, cant tu les vues coper, que li malaides faice rere son chief;	It is therefore necessary, when you have covered the artery, that patients make their face towards their head;
aprés li frotte lou leu d’un drapel aspre tant que les arteres aperent, puis estraingne li malaides son col a tout I drapel;	after rubbing the patient with an rough cloth until the arteries are visible, then extract the patient's neck from all the cloth;
puis regarde ou li voine bait, et li leus de l’une et de l’autre sont aprés les oreilles, et poc sont reponues;	Then look at where the vein is cut, and the veins of one are after the ears, and they are not returning;
puis signe les leus d’enche, puis cope l’une et l’autre d’un spatumile agut de II pars, tant que li taille veigne jusc’a l’os, et ceu soit par lou large dou chief.	Then sign the veins of the groin, then cut one and the other with a good spatula, two parts long, until the vein reaches the bone, so that it is near the width of the head.
Et se tu vues, boute le spatumile desoz l’artere et la cope au desus, en taillant ausi com II dois au traver.	If you see, pour out the spatumile under the artery and cut on top, in the same way as it should be cut through.
Et quant li voinne est copee, si saut li sans en haut continuelment fuers.	And when the vein is cut, if its blood flows without any upward continuity of fire.
Et se li artere n’apert au sentir, si covient que tu mesures la quantiteit de l’espaice de III dois, puis seigne d’enche et fent jusc’a l’os;	And if the arteries do not open at the feeling, it is wise to measure the quantity of the space three times larger, then sign the groin and cut until the bone.
et ceu qu’il covient dou sanc mettre fuers si est VI c/, et par aventure un poc plus ou moins, selonc ce que li malaides puet soffrir, et la repletion de l’artere;	and that which is advisable to put on a wound with fire if it is six times larger, and by chance a little more or less, according to what the patient can bear, and the replenishment of the artery.
puis regarde la plaie:	Then look at the wound:
s’il remaint sus l’os point dou syphac, si le cope que apostemes chaus n’i veigne, puis estrain la plaie et lie, et la cure d’oignement tant qu’ele soit sanee.	If the bone is still exposed under the flesh, then cut that which is pointed out as an abscess and drain the wound, and bind it up with cloth until it heals.
de emigrainne	Let goes
Quant emigrainne anciaine vient, et catarre agut, por les moistors des larmes et les chalors en temples et sode anciene forsenee et semblans choses, et il est medicinez par manieres de cures de medicine et tout ceu ne li profite mie, si estraions les arteres des temples et lou cauterizons, si com nos avons conteit.	When a head pain comes from old times, and cough is bad, because of moistness in the eyes and heat in the temples and an old forehead swelled up and similar things, if they are treated with medicines and all those cures don't help, then we extract the arteries from the temples and cauterize them, as we have told.
Et li maniere de l’estraction d’elles si est que li malaides faice rere les poilz de ses temples, et entende a l’artere qui apert en la temple, car elle apert bien par son batement, et est poc reponue fuers que en aucuns homes qui sont trop froit;	And the manner of their extraction, so that the patient makes his hair stand on end over his temples, and listens to the artery which opens in the temple, because it opens well with its pulsation, and is not very closed up until in many men who are too cold.
et s’elle est reponue, si estraigne son col li malaides d’aucuns drapelz, puis frote le leu d’aucun aspre drap, et arose le leu d’aigue chaude tant que li artere apere manifestement;	And if it is closed up, then strangle the neck of the patient with certain cloths, then rub him with any rough cloth, and pour water on him until the artery appears distinctly.
puis pren le spatumile de coi ci est li forme:	Then take the spatulate of which this is the form:
puis escorche le cuir legierement tant que tu veignes a l’artere, puis la trai en haut as pinceures, et la depart bien des toiles que sont desoz li de chescune partie;	Then scrape the soft skin lightly until you reach the artery, then tear it upwards with pins, and pull out well the threads that are on both sides of each part.
et se li artere est subtilz, si la torne a la pointe de l’uncine, puis la cope de celle partie selonc la quantiteit des II chiés.	and if the artery is subtle, then turn at the tip of the needle, and cut from that part according to the quantity of two heads.
Car s’elle n’est copee, si ne saut mie li sans dou tout en tout.	But if it is not cut, do not jump at it without causing damage all over.
Et trai dou sanc des VI c/, jusc’a III;	And pull out six times on each side, just three.
et se li artere est grans, si covient que tu la lies en II leus d’un fil double fort de soie, que porriture n’i veigne devant le soudement de la plaie, et veigne decorremens de sanc;	and if the artery is large, it is fitting that you tie two stitches of a strong double thread of silk, to prevent purulence in front of the sudden bleeding of the wound, and to come into view with the blood.
puis cope la superfluiteit qui est entre les II liiens en celle houre meisme, et puis, se tu vues, si lou cauterize dou cautere cutellaire jusc’a l’os tant que li chiés soient copez;	Then cut the swelling that is between the two joints on this same hour, and then, if you see, put the cautery of the surgical knife into the bone until the joint is cut.
et c’est li muedre oevre, se li malaides n’a fievre et il est de chaude complexion.	and that is the muscle work, if the patient does not have fever and has a hot complexion.
Car li cauteres est aide por finir les moistors:	For cauterization is a help to finish drying.
por ceu est il de plus grant aide as moistors.	because it is of greater help for drying.
Ou il covient por l’estraction des arteres que om emplisse lou leu de viel coton et mette on sus tentes bien faites;	Where it is necessary to extract the arteries, fill him with old cotton and put taut well-made tents.
et quant on les desliera, si soit curez de medicines seches que font naistre char, et de tentes, tant qu’il soit sanez;	and when you remove them, treat him with dry medicines that produce charcoal, and with tents, until he is healed.
et se sans cort de l’artere tant dis com tu i oevres, si te haste dou coper par cautere, ou tu emple lou leu de vitriole et l’estrain a ta main que li sans soit estainchiez;	And if without the cut of the artery so you do as you work, then hasten to cover by cautery, or apply the quick of vitriol and strain it with your hand until it is stained.
et se tu n’as ceu present, si met sor le leu ton doit tant que li sans soit congelez, et arose le leu d’aigue froide tant que li sans cesse, et soit estraint si com il covient;	And if you do not have that present, put the plaster on the shoulder until it is frozen, and apply the shoulder with cold water repeatedly, and strain it as needed.
et ceu qui est muedre et plus legier en l’estraction de l’artere est que tu cauterizes la voinne de cest cautere trenchant de II pars, mais li trenchant soient bien espés por warder plus longement lor chalor.	And what is muddied and easier to extract from the artery is that you should cauterize the vein of this cautery, cutting it with two halves, but cut them well spaced to make its heat last longer.
Car quant li estrumens est trop tenves, si tient moins sa chalor.	For when the instruments are too dark, they hold less their heat.
Et doit avoir entre les II coutelz I doit de gros d’espaice, et puis quant tu as signiet d’enche les II leus, et tu mes lou fer ardant sus tant qu’il viegne jusc’a l’os, et cope la voinne en II leus;	It must have one and a half inches of coarse iron between the two cuts, and when you have placed two sticks in it, and you heat the iron hot until it comes to the bone, cut the vein in two.
et soient esloigniet entre les II chiés car il n’est mie soudez de cest cautere dou tout en tout;	And let them separate between the two joints because it is not possible to solder all of this with fire in all of it;
et c’est li forme dou cautere:	and this is the form of the cauterization:
des larmes	from tears
